TITLE      De-excitation of Ni-58,60,62 compound nuclei formed    A0350001    3 
           via symmetric and asymmetric entrance channels         A0350001    4 
AUTHOR     (E.Bozek,D.M.De Castro-Rizzo,S.Cavallaro,B.Delaunay,   A0350001    5 
           J.Delaunay,H.Dumont,A.D'onofrio,M.G.Saint-Laurent,     A0350001    6 
           L.Sperduto,F.Terrasi)                                  A0350001    7 
REFERENCE  (J,NP/A,451,171,1986)                                  A0350001    8 
           (J,NP/A,427,151,1984) - technical details, part data   A0350001    9 
           on figures.                                            A0350001   10 
           (T,DECASTRO-RIZZO,1983) - in French, thesis,           A0350001   11 
           Orsay-Paris XI University (1983). Tables, technical    A0350001   12 
           details                                                A0350001   13 
INSTITUTE  (2FR SAC)                                              A0350001   14 
FACILITY   (VDGT,2FR SAC)                                         A0350001   15 
INC-SOURCE Beams of 12C, 18O, 28Si and 30Si were produced by the  A0350001   16 
           9 MV Van de Graaff tandem accelerator. Typical beam    A0350001   17 
           current of ~ 80 nA were used at the lowest bombarding  A0350001   18 
           energies, and ~ 20 nA at higher energies.              A0350001   19 
           A typical running time was - 6 h.                      A0350001   20 
DETECTOR   (GELI,HPGE) The gamma-rays were measured with two      A0350001   21 
           Ge(Li) and Ge(HP) detectors having efficiencies of     A0350001   22 
           22.3% and 23.9%, respectively, surrounded with a 10 cm A0350001   23 
           lead shield. These detectors were located at 90. and   A0350001   24 
           55. degr. (or 125. degr. for some measurements) with   A0350001   25 
           respect to the beam axis, at a distance of 10-15 cm    A0350001   26 
           from the target, in order to minimize summing effects. A0350001   27 
            The typical energy resolution was 2 keV FWHM for the  A0350001   28 
           1332 keV gamma-ray from a 60Co source.                 A0350001   29 
           Photopeak efficiencies were determined by placing      A0350001   30 
           calibrated sources (152Eu, 56Co, 57Co, 182Ta and       A0350001   31 
           133Ba) at the target position.                         A0350001   32 
ADD-RES    (COMP) Statistical model calculations.                 A0350001   33 
METHOD     (BCINT) The reaction chamber 100 mm in diameter made   A0350001   34 
           out of 0.4 mm thick stainless steel was kept at a      A0350001   35 
           pressure of 10**(-6) Torr, in order to reduce carbon   A0350001   36 
           buildup on the target. The chamber was electrically    A0350001   37 
           insulated from the beam line and used as a Faraday cup.A0350001   38 
           In the case of the 18O+44Ca reaction, another chamber, A0350001   39 
           allowing the handling of the target under vacuum in    A0350001   40 
           order to avoid oxydation of the calcium, was used.     A0350001   41 
           (GSPEC)                                                A0350001   42 
REL-REF    (D,,J.M.Alexander+,J,ZP/A,307,149,1982)                A0350001   43 
           (D,,T.D.Thomas+,J,ARN,18,543,1968)                     A0350001   44 
HISTORY    (19871012C)                                            A0350001   45 
           (20011012A) Several Subents were split according to    A0350001   46 
           EXFOR rules. Some reaction lines were corrected.       A0350001   47 
           Fusion and nonelastic data are added.                  A0350001   48 
           (20020520U) Last checking has been done.               A0350001   49 
           (20260323A) SD: Corrections in all Subents.            A0350001   50 
           CRITIQUE deleted (Gamma-ray transitions were added to  A0350001   51 
           appropriated Subents. Full description is given in     A0350001   52 
           thesis).                                               A0350001   53
